10b3(kha): gshen rab mchog de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par s+dzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'od kyi rgyal po gzi brjid rab tu 'bar ba'i mchog ces bya bas/ sems can rnams 
10b4(kha): 'tsho skyong ste/ de'i gdul ba'i zhing khams su / rgyal po'i khab g.yu lo ldan pa zhes bya ba der/ yab rgyal po don yod dpal dang / yum btsun mo khri gsal ma zhes bya ba gnyis 
10b5(kha): la/ sras gsum lam gnyis dang lnga ru bdog ste/ gcen po rgyal po yid bzhin mchog dang / de 'og legs pa'i mchog dang / gzung po rten chen mchog ces bya ba dang gsum 
10b6(kha): mo// lcam gnyis ni legs grub lcam dang / yid bzhin lcam zhes bya'o// de la rgyal bu yid bzhin mchog dang / btsun mo khri lcam ma zhes bya ba las/ rgyal bu dbang ldan / 
11a1(kha): zhes bya ba bdog go/ gzhan yang gzung po gnyis la/ btsun mon rgyung tham dang / ting btsun 'drul mo zhes bya ba yod d// gzhan yang tshing dpon gyi bu mo nar bu 
11a2(kha): bzang bo bya ba dang / dga' ba dage ldan ma zhes bya ba gnyis kyang / rgyal bu'i mdza' bo r yod d// gnan yang kblon poa drag byed dang / dpal 'byor dang / blo ldan dang / sgra mkhas 
11a3(kha): dang / rigs ldan dang / yid bzhin mchog dang / de rnams kyi dbag dang tshing dang khrims lasogs pa'i/ de dpon byed cing rgyal po'i chab srid skyong'o// gzhan yang 'khor dang longs 
11a4(kha): spyod dang / mnga'ras ni dpag tu med pa yod d// de la rgyal bu yid bzhin mchog gi zhal nas/ 'o skol rgyal s dam pa 'di dag na/ sngon chad gong ma'i mdzad srol ci ltar skyong / 
11a5(kha): bdag ni gzhan las dpag pa ma yin te/ gzhan la dpag par bya ba khyad par can/ gang dang mi 'dra ba zhig bya snyam na/ 'di' thabs dang blo gros ci ltar shim/ rgyal po dam pa

11b1(kha): po gang ma'i mdzad srol ni/ steng na gdugs bteg 'og na gdan kyang gnon/ mthon po'i dbu bcum dma' ba'i zhabs nas skyong / snang ba'i dgra 'dul byams pa'i gnyen kyang skyong / 
11b2(kha): rgyal slod nar sdzas longs spyod che bar bsgags/ rgyal po' bka' khrims rnams kyang gzung la nyan/ kun gyis smon pa 'gro ba gtsug gznod/ de bas che ba'i bya ba byed mi dgos/ 
11b3(kha): rgyal bus rgyal s gnon na rab ma yin/ pha mala bu yis zin na yang rab yin/ pha nor bu yis spyod na shes ldan yin/ so thub rangs zin na dpa' bo yin/ de phyir rgyal 
11b4(kha): po bya ba de gas tshog/ gzhan las de bas gang du dpag mi dgos/ zhes gsungaso// de la yum gyis smras pa/ gsen dang rgyal blon gtsi 'khor bcas pa rnams/ rgyal po yab sras

12b5(kha): yin/ rang mgo tsen pa rang btsa' 'dug zhes yin/ rang srog btsa' ba srnang po' bu zhig yin/ gzhan las ma dpag gang dang 'dra 'dra yin/ de pbyir dpag pa'i znor zhig e len lha/ 
12b6(kha): zhes zer ro// de la yang blon po sgra mkhan gyis gsol pa/ 'o skol rgyal po'i rgyal s dam pa 'dir/ gzhan las dpag pa'i bya ba byed snyam na/ gzhan la rgol ba rang gzhan 
13a1(kha): brlag 'dri yin/ zas zhir bsags pa rgyu ma mig brid yin/ 'jig rten 'di bden me rtag syu ma yin/ snang ba 'di ni skad cig gnha' prin yin/ m tshe 'di ni / 
13a2(kha): dara tsam su tsam yin/ phyi ma bya ba gtan gyis nam yin/ dge bslabs po che zhig spyod par 'bad/ byas pa bon la byas na don yod yin/ 'jig ten 'khor ba'i las spyod / 
13a3(kha): su yang mkhas/ de phyir thams cad dge la gzhol bar 'thad/ ces zer ro// de la yang blon po rig ldan gyis smras pa/ 'o skol rgyal po'i rgyals dam pa 'dir/ gzhan las 
13a4(kha): dpag pa'i bya ba byed snyam na/ byas pa dge dang stangs ma dgra lags te/ khyad par gzhan dag spyi las dpag pa yi/ lha klu'i rgyal po de la gnyen srid sbrel/ 'jig rten mi mo zhing 
13a5(kha): khams kun na yod/ lha klu'i sras mo yid bzhin nor dang mtshungs/ de yi rgyal rgyud ma chad gang las dpag/ 'gran gyis do med gtam dang rna la snyan/ tu gang gnyen la bskyel
